SAGE Labs earners, a new update is live!   We’ve made some changes to Faction Infrastructure Contracts. Check out the patch notes below! 👇  🔹 Each faction now gets 1 new recipe. The new recipe replaces Frameworks with Crystal Lattice and reduces the recipe value from SDUs.  🔹 FICs will now only refill when all sectors have no remaining buy orders. If one sector runs out but others still have orders, the empty sector will not be refilled until the rest are also depleted.  🔹 Each faction’s two FIC recipes will now spawn in 2 locations each (4 total per faction). These locations will be randomly re-assigned every Thursday at 17:00:00 UTC.  🔗: https://based.staratlas.com/

For those who haven’t noticed this yet @staratlas put out an economic dashboard on the governance site linked below. You can use this to check out local markets and see where all the volume is at and what items are in demand. Click on a Starbase hot spot and see all the demand there or click on a specific item and it’ll show you where the items are bought/sold the most at.   Team up this tool with @staratlasmaps where you can see the order book for each item at each starbase to see prices.   Mining and shipping back to css? Try seeing if there is demand for your resources at the hot spots in each faction or perhaps try to make a market for it. You can save on fuel from making less trips or increase your production by venturing out to the MRZ.   One example, hydrogen at MRZ 20 in Oni is in high demand and is selling for nearly the same as hydro at the CSS and hydrogen there has 50% more richness.   https://govern.staratlas.com/ecosystem-dashboard

Large discrepancies in price between markets provided opportunity for arbitrage.

## 2025-06-28 — SRC-X-STARATLAS-1939090749712408785

**Type:** Retweet / reshared context  
**URL:** https://x.com/staratlas/status/1939090749712408785  
**Engagement snapshot:** 0 likes; 95 reposts; 0 replies; 1 views

My best estimate is that we're very rapidly approaching the point of maximum capitulation on web3 gaming (and alts more broadly). Yes, it's been sad seeing the many studio closures over the year. I empathize with the losses people have experienced. And the loss in confidence in this new paradigm.  But I still believe gaming represents one of, if not the best use case for blockchain tech and crypto. There's a natural synergy with game economies, and real value ownership and capture. The quality teams (like Star Atlas) that have endured have not been resting on their laurels waiting for better market conditions. They've been building. They've been following their dream, and preparing themselves for releases, campaigns, and genuine sustainable growth. This consolidation to quality is going to lead to unfathomable success for those that have made it to this point.  Speaking for Star Atlas, I have incredible conviction that we are sitting on a powder keg. Our development velocity has only accelerated with time. We are positioned with game experiences catering to an insanely wide audience. We have a balanced and rewarding game economy that's been running smoothly for years. We have tokenomics with some of the best fundamentals I've seen in any web3 game. The smallest spark is going to ignite the engines, not to the moon, but to the next galaxy.  Until then, we keep grinding.

## 2025-08-15 — SRC-X-STARATLAS-1956579804595265898

**Type:** Retweet / reshared context  
**URL:** https://x.com/staratlas/status/1956579804595265898  
**Engagement snapshot:** 0 likes; 41 reposts; 0 replies; 0 views

Lot of posts out there today about Toly’s support of @ZinkSVM. And I get it. Feels like we’re leaving @solana. We’re not. We’ve deployed >25 onchain programs for Star Atlas. I would put our blockchain team against the best of any project on Solana. Many of those programs will continue to run on Solana. Our game systems need to shift.  I had calls with Toly and Raj in Q4 2020. I was convinced then that tech is the most scalable option. I still am. That’s why we picked SVM. Solana has seen incredible success over the past 5 years. That success has introduced some issues for us, which we intend to solve with http://z.ink.   But we’re extremely appreciative of the support that we’ve received over the years. And for many applications, Solana truly is the best.

I love it when a plan comes together.  Star Atlas is the world. @ZinkSVM is the agent execution layer. Together, they create the first crypto-native environment where AI agents can safely act as economic participants.  That is much stronger than “AI in a game.”  The stack:  Star Atlas = persistent economy Ships, land, fleets, resources, markets, factions, governance, player labor.,  AI agents = operators Fleet managers, market makers, faction coordinators, onboarding copilots, autonomous NPC/org actors, creator/business agents.,  http://z.ink / zProfile = permissioned execution, Agents need to act without holding private keys or asking for 500 signatures. zProfile lets users delegate bounded authority: asset limits, spending caps, actions, revocation, identity/reputation.  The investment thesis Crypto’s killer AI use case is not “chatbots with tokens.” It is permissioned autonomous economic activity.

I've had a friend, someone who I've known in the space for a super long time. They messaged asking if I was currently in a conference call this lovely scammer @RobtechGit said I was in/part of. I am not. I will never been in a random conference, I will always share on my socials if Im ever doing a podcast, talkshow etc.   Don't Download links from people on the internet asking you to join a call,  Do not link any wallets or anything like that  Do not sign anything Don't interact with random drops   DO always be super careful in these situations and research  I don't know what this person is attempting to do but I am not part of this, I am not in this conference and I doubt some of the others showing as being there are actually them, they most likely took our profile pictures to lure people in.
